<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e4d6bfe3-996c-48df-b17d-99cbd9cfdea3'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

  <span id="freeText4400389703807105351" style="display:none"><i>Two worlds of wealth and passion call to Nora Sutherlin and, whichever one she chooses, it will be the hardest decision she will ever have to make. Unless someone makes it for her…</i><br /><br />Wes Railey is the object of Nora's tamest yet most maddening fantasies, and the one man she can't forget. He's young. He's wonderful. He's also thoroughbred royalty and, reuniting with him in Kentucky, she's in his world now. But this infamous New York dominatrix is no simpering Southern belle, and Nora's dream of fitting into Wesley's world is perpetually at odds with the relentlessly seductive pull of Søren—her owner, her lover, the forever she cannot have. At least, not completely.<br /><br />Meanwhile Nora's associate Kingsley Edge is only too happy to take her place at Søren's feet during her hiatus. Søren is the only man Kingsley has ever loved, and their dark, shared history has forged a bond that neither the years—nor Søren's love for Nora—can break. But a new threat from an old adversary is forcing Kingsley to confront the past, reminding him that he must keep his friends close, and his enemies closer.</span>

<div id="bookReviews">
  




  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1255011839" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1255011839" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1255011839?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1255011839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17743066220574509177"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED :::</b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429236868i/14556659.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> **** GASPPP!!!!! **** Holyyyyyy SHIT!!! OMG. Ahhh!!! The ending of this book made my heart STOP!!!! </b><br/><br/>I am so freaking glad that the next book is already out because I NEED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENS! Gah. This series is putting me through the wringer but I totally love it and I can't stop reading!!<br/><br/>Note: This is the third book in a series that <u>must</u> be read in order. This review is pretty safe for anyone, but you should read <i>The Siren</i> and <i>The Angel</i>  before this book.<br/><br/>If you'</span>
  <span id="freeText17743066220574509177" style="display:none"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED :::</b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429236868i/14556659.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> **** GASPPP!!!!! **** Holyyyyyy SHIT!!! OMG. Ahhh!!! The ending of this book made my heart STOP!!!! </b><br><br>I am so freaking glad that the next book is already out because I NEED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENS! Gah. This series is putting me through the wringer but I totally love it and I can't stop reading!!<br><br>Note: This is the third book in a series that <u>must</u> be read in order. This review is pretty safe for anyone, but you should read <i>The Siren</i> and <i>The Angel</i>  before this book.<br><br>If you've already read the first two books, you'll naturally have a <em>ton</em> of questions stored up about all the various character and (thankfully) this is a book of <em>answers</em>. There's a lot of back story mixed in with two present day storylines that together fill in so many blanks. I'm really in awe of how multi-layered this story is. Between that and the incredible writing, it's really a series that is hard to put down.<br><br>The story in this book is split into three interconnected parts: Søren &amp; Kingsley's past thirty years ago in the Jesuit school they both attended, Søren &amp; Kingsley's present day activities as they search for the elusive thief that is threatening them, and Nora &amp; Wesley in present day time together down in Kentucky.<br><br>I really feel like, even though I've liked Søren up until this point, I've also been a little wary of him. He's a sadist -- a man who can only be sexually aroused by causing pain or humiliation to his lover. That freaks me out a little. What keeps him a good man is that he has a conscience. Everything he engages in is consensual so he's not a monster. But it just makes me uncomfortable... That being said, there's also a lot more to him than just his sexual preferences. And that was what we learned in this book.<br><br>This man had given up everything he had to God, except the part of his heart that would always belong to Eleanor. He's such an enigma. He inspires love from his congregation, respect merely by his nature from anyone who meets him, and abject fear (and awe) from the Underground. But learning about his past really did help me to understand that despite his <em>need </em>for sexual sadism, undearneath that was a very, very good man (as Nora has told us so many times). He's kind, selfless, and caring. But he's also like the eye of a storm -- borderline lethal and deadly calm. A sadist with a conscience and a good heart.<br><br>And we <em>finally</em> get to learn oh-so-much more about Kingsley. This man -- King of the Underground, top Dom only below Søren -- had a whole other side to him that few people knew about. His tale is honestly rather heartbreaking (even to where it's at now) -- the ultimate unrequited love... almost tragically so.<br><br>I loved seeing the way the layers of their histories come together through their shared mutual bond, desires, and close connection at such an early age. Best friends and mortal enemies -- the deepest of love mixed with the deepest of hate. It was honestly fascinating to see the two most dominant men of the Underground world show such private vulnerabilities with regards to each other -- something they'd kept  hidden from those around them. Over thirty years of shared history and yet so many unresolved feelings.<br><br>For the first time I began to see Søren in a different light -- and appreciate how isolating his way of being was, and the incredible lengths he went through to protect those around him from himself.<br><br>Meanwhile, miles away, Nora returns home with Wesley to him home in Kentucky. Sweet, sweet Wesley -- so in love with her, and the only man to ever love her without hurting her first. I love them together <em>so much!!!!</em> Everything about them just fills my heart to bursting with FEELS. Even though they're complete opposites, they just feel so right to me. And the WAY he loves he just breaks my heart. -- <em>“When Søren hurts you, I die inside.”</em> -- Gah!!!!! I loved they way they were both fumbling around in new waters together even though their situations were vastly different -- her, a world-reknown dominatrix who'd never had vanilla sex without kink, and him, a virgin who was saving himself for the woman he loved. They were so cute! Ahhh, her learning to cuddle. *clutches heart* Not going to lie though, I am worried as to whether or not they'll genuinely be able to make it work. I do worry. Even though I am rooting for them.<br><br><i>Although</i>, I admittedly have warmed up to Søren <em>enough</em> that I am now just a teensy bit torn. But like, what kind of future could he offer her? I feel like he was an integral part of her past... and will probably always be a part of her for the rest of her life... but I also feel like Wesley is her future. Is it horrible of me to kinda want her to end up with Wesley but maybe have him be okay with her going to be with Søren every now and again?? Hehe. Ok. Yeah, maybe that's too far. *sigh* Maybe after reading three of these books, I'm adopting the whole "no boundaries" outlook of this world a little too much. Don't judge.<br><br>I JUST WANT EVERYONE TO BE HAPPY!!! *flails*<br><br>I have to say I'm beyond impressed with the way this author kept these three storylines going at the same time without ever making it confusing and simultaneously making you feel invested in all of them.<br><br>This series has the ability to be incredibly intense one moment, then keep you on the edge of your seat with the dangerous tension, then be scandalously kinky, incredibly romantic and tender, and then have you laugh out loud the next. There's witty banter, deep theology, complex plotlines, and heart-wrenching emotions.<br><br>I really have come to love and respect/understand the way there's just no limitations to the "who" or "how" of the love in this series. It's just love. Plain and simple. The circumstances and details are irrelevant. Love can happen anywhere and in so many different forms. Only the love itself matters.<br><br>This entire series has a kind of storytelling that is one of my favorites where not only is there one big story arc, but each chapter has it's own smaller, but equally profound arc, such that the last words of each chapter always hold great meaning. They have *ooooomph*, y'know? Meaning. Power. I love it!<br><br>So yeah, #TeamSøren people... for the first time in this series, I'm actually starting to feel a little torn. Not that I want her to be with Søren, but I get why she's so attached to him. I really do. Honestly it was the '100 ways' and 'spider' things that made me warm up to him the most. I guess also by seeing his past, it's a little easier for me to separate his sadism from who he is as a person. <em>But</em> it just really does bother me that he <em>cannot</em> get aroused without causing pain to his lover. I'm sorry, but as good a man as he is, that bothers me. So, I'm #TeamSøren in the sense that I like his character and I want him to be happy.... but if I had to pick Nora's HEA, I'm #TeamWesley. I just love the way he loves her. So much. *sniff*<br><br>For new readers, please note that this is an erotic series, but it's not a romance even though there is very deep, strong, and true LOVE within the story. Overall, it's very boundary pushing and non-traditional, so it might not be the series for everyone (it took me <em>years</em> to work up to reading them), but I would suggest giving them a try because even though they're almost the complete opposite of what I normally would think I'd want to read, I am totally LOVING this series! <em>Loving it!</em><br><br>On to the next book!! :D<br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5 stars. Contemporary erotica.</strong><br>(I dont know if I should mark 4 or 5 stars... still undecided.)<br><br>My review of book #1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1I3176u">http://bit.ly/1I3176u</a><br>My review of book #2: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1JIzQay">http://bit.ly/1JIzQay</a><br>________________________________________<br><br><b>SERIES READING ORDER: </b><br>Book #1: The Siren <br>Book #2: The Angel<br>Book #3: The Prince<br>Book #4: The Mistress<br>Book #5: The Saint<br>Book #6: The King<br>Book #7: The Virgin<br>Book #8: The Queen<br>________________________________________<br><br><b>FAVORITE QUOTES:</b><br>Note: I “hid” these in a spoiler tag but they’re not really spoilers. I only hid them because there are a lot and I thought it would be annoying to just have them out there. It would be best if you read the first two books first I think, but there’s nothing in here that’s overly revealing. It’s about as safe as quotes from a third book in a series can be. Take a look if you want :)<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>He wanted to sleep for days, for years even. Maybe when he woke up he would be a grown man and no one would send him away again. The day would come when he would take orders from no one, and that would be the best day of his life.<br>________________________<br><br>Up close, he appeared not only more handsome than before, but strangely inscrutable. He seemed like a book, shut tight and locked in a glass box, and Kingsley would have done anything for the key. He met the young man’s eyes and saw no kindness in those steely gray depths. No kindness, but no cruelty, either. He inhaled in nervousness as the pianist passed him, and smelled the unmistakable scent of winter.<br>________________________<br><br>Her grunts and cries of pain and fear were the sweetest sounds he could imagine. Only they could silence the music in his ears that he heard from the time he woke until he fell asleep and into blissful oblivion again. One piano concerto thirty years ago… and still he couldn’t unheard it…<br>________________________<br><br>He died while inside her and he cherished that death, that freedom, those few seconds when he was released from the spell of the only man in the Underground who wore a collar but belonged to no one.”<br>________________________<br><br>She’d joked her motto was Have Riding Crop, Will Travel…. And for her own safety she relied on only two things — her notoriety as the most dangerous Domme in the world, and Kingsley’s reputation as the last man in America anyone wanted to cross.<br>________________________<br><br>Wesley grinned down at her and her heart knotted up in her chest. God damn, she had missed this kid — so fucking much that being back with him almost hurt as much as letting him go had.<br>________________________<br><br>“Now if you’ll excuse m, I need to get back to my Portuguese.”<br>“You’re learning Portuguese, too?” Kingsley asked. “How many languages do you speak?”<br>“Eight.”<br>“I’m bilingual. What do they call someone like you?”<br>Stearns arched an eyebrow at him. “Intelligent.”<br>________________________<br><br>“Can I take a moment here to tell you both how cute your accents are when you’re angry?”<br>Wesley and his father both looked at her, Wesley in shock, his father in disgust.<br>“Okay, that’s a ‘no’ then. Carry on.”<br>________________________<br><br>Nora was lawless, unmanageable, uncontrollable. You told her one thing, she did everything but that. She laughed when others cried. Danced when others sat. She clawed her way to the top and didn’t even chip a nail on the way up. No one could break her. No one could handle her. No one could shut her up.<br>God, he had missed this woman.<br>________________________<br><br>Soren seemed to delight in intense eye contact. He could read someone with a single glance — know their motives, their plans, what they wanted, who they trusted… As teenagers, Kingsley had thought it was a great parlour trick. It wasn’t until years later… that he understood the root of Soren’s talent. Abused children often grew up with extraordinarily astute abilities to judge character. It wasn’t a gift. It wasn’t a parlour trick. It was life or death, a survival skill.<br>________________________<br><br>“I pray for you, Kingsley.”<br>Kingsley grinned. “Pray harder.”<br>________________________<br><br>The intimacy of his touch resonated deep within her. Some part of her had missed this… whatever it was, this tenuousness in him, this respect she felt in his hands, on his lips. He was careful with her. That was it. He touched her as if he worried he’d break her. <br>She’d never been with a man who hadn’t wanted to break or be broken by her.<br>________________________<br><br>“You aren’t afraid of me right now.” A statement, not a question, and yet Kingsley heard the question underneath the words. ‘Why?’<br>There’s nothing you could do to me now that I wouldn’t want.”<br>________________________<br><br>“Stop staring at me, Kingsley,” Soren said as he turned his eyes from the road outside the window to Kingsley’s face.<br>“I’ve been staring at your for thirty years. You should be used to it by now, mon ami.”<br>________________________<br><br>Soren had wanted to own this girl.<br>He’d fallen in love with her instead. And whether she realized it or not, because of his love for her, she owned him as much as he owned her.”<br>________________________<br><br>“What are you praying for, mon ami?” Kingsley had asked.<br>“What I’ve been praying for every day since I met you,” Stearns said, twisting the beads around his hand.<br>“And what is that?”<br>Stearns opened his hand to display the rosary beads he’d weaved between his fingers like a spiderweb.<br>“Strength.”<br>________________________<br><br>“My name is Soren.”<br>________________________<br><br>Soren glared at him. “We’re not having the Saint Peter’s Basilica argument again.”<br>“I’m getting you a pair of red leather shoes for Christmas. Why should the Pope have all the fun.”<br>“I miss beating you sometimes, Kingsley. I truly do.”<br>________________________<br><br>He ran so Soren would chase him. He ran because he wanted to be taken. He ran hard and ran fast, yes. But not as hard and fast as he could.<br>________________________<br><br>“When Soren hurts you, I die inside.”<br>________________________<br><br>“It is better to be feared than loved.<br>Kingsley heard the sorrow in Soren’s voice, the longing for something he thought he couldn’t have.<br>“And…” Soren continued, “It’s safer to be feared than loved. At least where I’m concerned.” He smiled almost shyly and Kingsley suddenly understood it all — why Soren was so cold, so remote, why he could and did install such fear in the hearts of everyone who came near him. He did it on purpose. He did it to keep them safe.<br>________________________<br><br>Some sadists took years learning to master the art of inflicting pain without causing hard. But Soren was a natural. He was fluent in nineteen modern languages, five ancient languages and the one true universal language — pain.<br>________________________<br><br>“I still love you as I did that night you broke me.”<br>________________________<br><br>“Let me tell you a little secret…” She held him by the chin and turned his eyes up to her. “I’m no romance-novel heroine. I might even be the villain.”<br>________________________<br><br>Sadist. They left their notches not on their lovers’ bedposts but on the very bodies of those who braved their beds.<br>________________________<br><br>“I feel like I could do anything I wanted today.”<br>“Welcome to the afterglow. It’s nice, right?”<br>“Very. They should sell this stuff on the black market.”<br>“They do. It’s called pot.”<br>________________________<br><br>“I want to name a horse.”<br>“If you stay here, you can name all the horses from now on.”<br>________________________<br>Wesley’s love… it seemed so strange to her, so novel. Where had it come from? And why? She would understand the origin of the stars before she ever got why this beautiful boy, so sweet and pure, would love a woman like her.”<br>________________________<br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/subscribe/" rel="nofollow noopener">Subscribe by email</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer687906399" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4559206675399537517"><strong>Nora, Who??? </strong><br/><br/>This series just keeps getting better! Delving further into Soren and Kingsley's shared past was quite enlightening. These two really stole the show in this book. I have a whole new perspective now, and a lot more questions. All I'll say is, Poor Kingsley! He really got a rough deal. No pun intended.<br/><br/>I'm still struggling with trying to like Soren. I'm just not seeing the overwhelming goodness that keeps being referenced with regard to him. He had some terrible things happen to him ea</span>
  <span id="freeText4559206675399537517" style="display:none"><strong>Nora, Who??? </strong><br /><br />This series just keeps getting better! Delving further into Soren and Kingsley's shared past was quite enlightening. These two really stole the show in this book. I have a whole new perspective now, and a lot more questions. All I'll say is, Poor Kingsley! He really got a rough deal. No pun intended.<br /><br />I'm still struggling with trying to like Soren. I'm just not seeing the overwhelming goodness that keeps being referenced with regard to him. He had some terrible things happen to him early in life. I get it. I'm just not sure that excuses many of his own deplorable acts. Then again, that is what makes him such a compelling character.<br /><br />Admittedly, I was initially rolling my eyes at the idea of Nora running away from Soren and back to sweet Wesley. I mean, really! How long is she going to string this poor guy along? We all knew that in all likelihood she'd never completely walk away from Soren. So yeah, I wasn't thrilled with where things left off at the end of the last book.<br /><br />However, this book had my rapt attention in no time. With mysterious threats and a sordid forbidden love story, I couldn't have cared less about what was going on with Nora and her boy-toy. It was a little distracting to bounce back and forth so much, but it kept me on the edge of my seat the entire time. Having the sweet and innocent story of Nora and Wes alternated with the darker love story of Soren and Kingsley also provided a little reprieve from some intense scenes.<br /><br />Overall, this was an intense and suspenseful read. With a huge cliffhanger ending, I expect to see Nora take a more central role in the book that follows. I will be diving into the next book in this series immediately. What a wild, kinky ride!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4559206675399537517" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer574028741" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15239211376895380991"><br/><br/><b>***PLS DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW IF YOU HAVEN’T READ THIS SERIES, WHAT A SHAME BY THE WAY!***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379790693i/540429._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Tiffany did it again. I used to think Nora was based on her but now I am pretty sure she is more Soren-ish. Poor Andrew, he must be Kingsley!<br/>This book starts just after The Angel. As you might remember Nora was running off (cruel bitch) to meet boring Wesley and Soren was left alone (no worries Sir, I will always be here for you).<br/><br/>This is two books in one, maybe three books in one and let me explain you why</span>
  <span id="freeText15239211376895380991" style="display:none"><br><br><b>***PLS DO NOT READ THIS REVIEW IF YOU HAVEN’T READ THIS SERIES, WHAT A SHAME BY THE WAY!***</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379790693i/540429._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tiffany did it again. I used to think Nora was based on her but now I am pretty sure she is more Soren-ish. Poor Andrew, he must be Kingsley!<br>This book starts just after The Angel. As you might remember Nora was running off (cruel bitch) to meet boring Wesley and Soren was left alone (no worries Sir, I will always be here for you).<br><br>This is two books in one, maybe three books in one and let me explain you why. We get to meet young Soren &amp; Kingsley, we get to know more about adults Soren &amp; Kingsley and we get to deflower boring Wes.<br><br><b>NORTH – PAST &amp; PRESENT</b><br>Young Soren is scary, like these guys who don’t speak with anyone at all. He’s always playing his piano, always with his thoughts until Kingsley arrives to his school.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415286ra/819761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kingsley is a womanizer, typical hot French guy with hot accent who always gets what he wants. But this time he wants Soren, he feels an special attraction that he can’t deny and he wants to submit to him at any cost.<br><br>In this book we get to know Kingsley better. He has feelings and I think it was my favourite character in The Prince. Tiffany Reisz is able to make you love or hate a character, no matter the idea you had about them before. <br><br>While we’re getting some information about their younger life together, we also see how Kingsley’s love for Soren is still there and I doubt that is gonna disappear anytime soon. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”I’ve ben in love with a ghost for thirty years”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I felt like their love is the real one, like they are meant to be together during all the book. And I also felt Soren loves Kingsley. He married Kingsley’s sister to spend more time with him, that is LOVE. I know I thought Nora and Soren were meant to be together but I was wrong. Soren and Kingsley have been together for thirty years, they have been best friends, like brothers, they have been lovers, Soren made all he could to make Kingsley the man he is now. I know Reisz has no idea what a HEA means but I seriously need them to end up together somehow!<br><br><b>SOUTH </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415286i/819762.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok, I admit it. I like Wesley! Happy? I really hope Soren is not reading this because he’s going to spank my arse, not that I wouldn’t enjoy that!.<br><br>Wesley might be the man for Nora. I am not pretty sure if she can be happy being vanilla (well, wall sex is not vanilla, right?) BUT she should try so she leaves Soren alone.<br><br>We get to meet Wesley’s world. Rich world to be exact. That guy has a palace or something like that in Kentucky with horses, lots of them. And let’s say his parent is not exactly a fan of Nora and her smart ass comments.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”I know who you are, Miss Sutherlin.”<br>“A fan? How nice.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>I don’t really want to talk about K&amp;S or N&amp;W stories because you can read the books and I will never EVER make this any justice but I want to say a few things about our lovely <s>sadist</s> author.<br><br>I felt I was reading REAL relationships and I need all authors to take note on this. That scene where Wesley popped his cherry was SO DAMN REAL! Because in real life, when you lose your virginity is SHIT! But authors want you to think that losing your virginity is the best thing you can experience. HELL NO! If you’re lucky, after a few times you will start having fun but NOT definitely the first time. And yes, people have morning breath, I thought it was just me after all those cheesy books!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415286i/819763.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me finish this with some thoughts about The Mistress… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I don't know what's gonna happen with that crazy French girl, why is she alive??? I was NOT expecting that bitch to show up!!! I really really really hope K&amp;S will end up together, I don’t know how this is going to end but I need them together somehow. I would love to see a kinky Wes but I don’t know if that’s even possible. <br>And then, they say Grace will have an important role, I don't want to think that she new about Marie Laure all this time because I'd kill that bitch and will keep Zach all to myself!<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br><b>READ THIS BOOK, that is all</b><br><br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7791834357812483043">You have to read the books by breaking them up, gives you the pleasure of reading 3 books and not one!<br/>North - Past first<br/>Then North - Present <br/>Then South<br/><br/>Ahhh, I absolutely loveeeeee this series. Time to grab and re-read book 4!<br/>~<br/><br/><br/>All I can say is,<br/><br/>What. A. Book<br/>What. A. Fucking. Brilliantly. Amazing. Book.<br/>Giving it 5 Stars is giving it far too little.<br/><br/><br/>In this book 'The Prince', we learn and read about two Prince, 'The Prince of Kentucky' and 'La Petit Prince.'<br/><br/>First I was all<br/>￼<br/><br/>Then, at the end I was like</span>
  <span id="freeText7791834357812483043" style="display:none">You have to read the books by breaking them up, gives you the pleasure of reading 3 books and not one!<br />North - Past first<br />Then North - Present <br />Then South<br /><br />Ahhh, I absolutely loveeeeee this series. Time to grab and re-read book 4!<br />~<br /><br /><br />All I can say is,<br /><br />What. A. Book<br />What. A. Fucking. Brilliantly. Amazing. Book.<br />Giving it 5 Stars is giving it far too little.<br /><br /><br />In this book 'The Prince', we learn and read about two Prince, 'The Prince of Kentucky' and 'La Petit Prince.'<br /><br />First I was all<br />￼<br /><br />Then, at the end I was like<br />￼<br />￼<br /><br />I've got absolutely no words. Amazing and Brilliant are not the words you can use while saying how good this book was, This book needs a new word to describe it.<br />Actually, This series needs a new word appart from fantastic, brilliant, amazing etc to describe it. Someone go invent a better word.. lol<br />'The Original Sinners' is hands down, one of the best series I have ever read.<br />Each and every dialogue sends a shiver down the spine when you read them because they hold that weight and you feel it while reading it. I wish these characters were real!!<br /><br />The book is sheer brilliant, You learn so much about Kingsley, Søren, Nora and Wesley and more!!<br />The ending left me with my jaw hitting the floor, all in terror and surprise and just HOLY FUCKING SHIT, Someone slap me and say it isn't true because I'm freaking the shit out.<br /><br />You can read the book two ways, First read all the South stuff, which is about Nora and Wesley and then Read the North stuff which is divided into Kingsley and Søren's past and future. Or read them all together. hehe, I like a dip shit read South first, then North. Felt like I was reading two amazing books instead of one. *grins*<br />While reading North Past, We learn so so so so much about Kingsley and Søren's past, about how they were in the same school, how they became lovers and how everything worked out between them and how did they land up the way they are today. In the North Present, we see how Kingsley and Søren are finding the 'someone' and so help me god when they did, I got a heart attack. Back in the South, the story of Wesley and Nora continue, How he will do anything to keep her! Does Nora belong to Wesley or Søren? Who will she land up with? ;) Don't you just want to read it to find out?<br /><br />The book is written with such perfection, Tiffany Reisz is really something. Hats off you you Tiffany Reisz, This is one of the best stories I've ever read in the narration, reading, story, character's, plot etc's pov!<br /><br />Cannot wait for 2013 and read the 4# book!! Like seriously, Its going to be torturous!!!<br /><br />One thing the book taught me was<br /><br />"Not to ask questions we don't want the answers to"<br /><br /><br />"You said my safe word." - Søren<br />[I fell in love with him a 100 times more.]<br /><br /><br />READ THE BOOK.<br /><br />Have you ever been high on a book? Well I have, Its an amazing feeling.. Its like your on some book crack! Very few books can give you that doze. Got me so high! <br /><br />ARC courtesy of Harlequin via NetGalley</span>

<div id="review_389628754" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/389628754" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/389628754?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=bdsm-or-person-in-control">bdsm-or-person-in-control</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=dark-or-taboo">dark-or-taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer389628754" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3150644185670424902"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380387311i/747302.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><u>Excerpt from 'Two Princes' by the Spindoctors</u><br/><br/>But I know what a prince and lover ought to be <br/>I know what a prince and lover ought be</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>4.5 stars. This is the story of <i>The Prince of Kentucky</i> and <i>The King who started out as 'La Petit Prince.'</i><br/><br/>My favorite of the series so far. The writing was flawless, the suspense was taken up a notch, and some of the characters' secrets were finally starting to spill out from the shadows. <br/><br/>While I thought the poking-fun-at-romance-books segment was a bit ov</span>
  <span id="freeText3150644185670424902" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380387311i/747302.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><u>Excerpt from 'Two Princes' by the Spindoctors</u><br><br>But I know what a prince and lover ought to be <br>I know what a prince and lover ought be</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>4.5 stars. This is the story of <i>The Prince of Kentucky</i> and <i>The King who started out as 'La Petit Prince.'</i><br><br>My favorite of the series so far. The writing was flawless, the suspense was taken up a notch, and some of the characters' secrets were finally starting to spill out from the shadows. <br><br>While I thought the poking-fun-at-romance-books segment was a bit overdone (although quite true!), the point was driven home that this story is dark, honest, raw, full of heart, and <i>not</i> your typical romance. I'd said in my review for the last book, <i>The Angel</i>, that some of the words Reisz puts on the page would serve well as an advertisement for BDSM. This book continued with more of the same message :<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"That's not what I'm talking about. I'm not talking about collars and leashes and leads. When you love somebody, they own you whether you're kinky or not."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I was happy to get some of the answers regarding Kingsley's and Soren's backstory, and why there was some lingering animosity between the two of them. In fact, I ended up enjoying their portion of the story much more than I enjoyed what was going on with Wes and Nora. Soren continues to become more and more human to me, which I appreciate. <br><br>Nora...sigh. I keep hoping that one of these books I'm going to start warming up to this character more. However, I still feel like I <i>know nothing about her</i> other than she loves to write, is easy on the eyes, wears cute pajamas, has a shitty social filter, and wants to seduce the pants off every man she comes in contact with...especially the ones who are challenges. With every new man who gets added to the story, we see yet another person who wants to have her in one way or another. It's just getting old to me. I'd really love to see another woman up in this mix as a main character to balance those scales a little bit. Does such a world exist where one woman gets to keep all of her past and present lovers close, with no real outside female interference? And I'm not talking about the crazy psycho kind, I'm talking real life petty stuff.<br><br>My one big complaint that has to be spoiler tagged : WTF was up with Nora talking to Wesley <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[about the ways that she had sex with Soren WHILE THEY WERE HAVING SEX? Is that really the time to have such a conversation, while you're being penetrated by another man? And it HAPPENED MORE THAN ONCE! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I'm not saying that the conversation couldn't have come up, but couldn't it have happened during a more appropriate time? Those moments made my head hurt and totally killed part of the book for me.<br><br>That said, this is still my favorite book of the series. Each installment drags me deeper into the world of The Original Sinners and makes me only want to know more. This is literary erotica brought to an art form, and I'm glad that I stuck with the series and gave it a second chance after being on the fence with the first book. The effort was worth the reward.<br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1893118177" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9590666855127299120"><b>RATING: 5+++++ Destined Hearts!! <3 <3</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Time stopped. The world ended. No one noticed except Kingsley. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>WOW. Just WOW. I am wrecked and in awe of Ms. Reisz' phenomenal, lyrical writing and her equally, if not more, breathtaking world and characters. I am lost in my emotions because after this, I wholeheartedly know and believe that Søren, Kingsley, and Wes own me, heart, mind, body and soul. And there is nothing I can do or say to change that. Their story cannot and will not be underst</span>
  <span id="freeText9590666855127299120" style="display:none"><b>RATING: 5+++++ Destined Hearts!! &lt;3 &lt;3</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Time stopped. The world ended. No one noticed except Kingsley. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />WOW. Just WOW. I am wrecked and in awe of Ms. Reisz' phenomenal, lyrical writing and her equally, if not more, breathtaking world and characters. I am lost in my emotions because after this, I wholeheartedly know and believe that Søren, Kingsley, and Wes own me, heart, mind, body and soul. And there is nothing I can do or say to change that. Their story cannot and will not be understood unless it is experienced, first hand. In order to revel in it and drown in its feelings, you must simply read it.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I hated how you stared at me.” Søren raised his hand and laid it on Kingsley’s shoulder. He moved his hand up Kingsley’s neck and pressed his thumb into the hollow of his throat.<br />“And why is that?”<br />“Because,” Søren said, bending his regal head the four inches that separated them, “it made it impossible for me to stare back.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Søren and Kingsley: these two broken men, soulmates in every sense and star-crossed lovers need to end up together. I don't care how, they just do.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Je suis le vôtre. J’étais toujours le vôtre, monsieur.”<br />I am yours. I have always been yours, sir. <br />“Oui. Tu es le mien.” <br />Yes, you are mine. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />I loved <i>The Angel</i>, but I worship <i>The Prince</i>. No words can completely describe my soul-deep feelings for this book, but to simply put it <i>Many Waters...</i><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Posted: January 29, 2017</i>

<div id="review_1140671480" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1140671480" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1140671480?book_show_action=true">Dec 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6285155-eda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1140671480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13847166942354942963"><br/><b>
  <i>** 5++ “<u>the scent of pine and winter</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve always wanted to believe God made me this way for a reason.”<br/><br/>“Je suis la raison.”<br/><u>I am the reason.</u></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419566787ra/13093159.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I just finished the book and here I am, in awe, in shock and terribly afraid to learn what’s going to happen next!<br/><br/><b>WHAT KIND OF MOTHERF*CKING CLIFFHANGER IS THAT?!?</b> If I didn’t already have <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17251444.The_Mistress__The_Original_Sinners___4_' title='The Mistress (The Original Sinners, #4) by Tiffany Reisz' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Mistress</a>, I’d go crazy for sure.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4480131.Tiffany_Reisz' title='Tiffany Reisz' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tiffany Reisz</a>, you have a black heart, you evil woman! :P<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419567051ra/13093178.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First of all, I have to admit the fact that I couldn’t</span>
  <span id="freeText13847166942354942963" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 5++ “<u>the scent of pine and winter</u>” STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve always wanted to believe God made me this way for a reason.”<br><br>“Je suis la raison.”<br><u>I am the reason.</u></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419566787ra/13093159.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just finished the book and here I am, in awe, in shock and terribly afraid to learn what’s going to happen next!<br><br><b>WHAT KIND OF MOTHERF*CKING CLIFFHANGER IS THAT?!?</b> If I didn’t already have <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17251444.The_Mistress__The_Original_Sinners___4_" title="The Mistress (The Original Sinners, #4) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mistress</a>, I’d go crazy for sure.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4480131.Tiffany_Reisz" title="Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">Tiffany Reisz</a>, you have a black heart, you evil woman! :P<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419567051ra/13093178.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First of all, I have to admit the fact that I couldn’t care less about <b>Nora</b> and <b>Wesley</b>’s chapters. All the horses and catfish and cherry poppin’ was, in fact, <b>BORING AS HELL</b>. I’m not even going to comment on anything about them. They’re happy. They love each other. Everything’s great.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419567494ra/13093225.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's common knowledge that I’ve been drooling over and swooning for <b>Søren</b> since reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10970532.The_Siren__The_Original_Sinners___1_" title="The Siren (The Original Sinners, #1) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">The Siren</a> and he’s been the highlight of the last 2 books for me.<br><br><i>Not anymore, though</i>.<br><br><b>Kingsley Edge</b> has pushed him aside, took his crown and sat on the throne in my heart, <i>gloriously.</i> I have never in my life been sucked so potently into the story of a man's undying love. I have never in my life felt so broken for a character in a book. My heart constricted with every word of affection leaving Kingsley’s lips and with every harsh sentence he needed to hear coming out of Søren’s. <i>I have never in my life rooted for a couple to “make it”, this deeply.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“What are you praying for, mon ami?”<br><br>“What I’ve been praying for every day since I met you.”<br><br>“And what is that?”<br><br>“<u>Strength.</u>”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>A very young Kingsley falls hopelessly in love with the cold and terrifyingly calm <b>Mr. Stearns</b>, over notes of Ravel coming from a piano in the chapel, the scent of pine and winter and the Christian cross that he tore from his neck, in the halls of St. Ignatius Catholic Boarding School. While Søren’s love is brutal, violent and torturous, Kingsley’s devotion, longing and despair is breathtakingly beautiful.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Heaven was now, this moment underneath Stearns. Hell had been every moment before and would be every moment after.<br>~KINGSLEY</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419566787ra/13093160.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Kingsley has not been released from the spell of the steely gray eyes of the only man in the Underground <i>who wore a collar but belonged to no one</i>, <b>for the last thirty years.</b> He still can not stop staring at Søren, just like when he first laid eyes on him. He is still in love with the ghost of the man that once broke him and built him up to break him all over again, everyday. <i>But all he can do is lap up the crumbs of love Søren occasionally throws at his feet, while trying to hate him.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Don’t hate her. It’s me who hurt you. Hate me.”<br><br>“Don’t worry, mon ami. <u>I do.</u>”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Kingsley and Søren’s love, I think, is what destiny is. I <b>need</b> them to end up together! I don’t care about anyone else in the story, <i>as long as these two tortured but perfect men decide to pick each other for eternity</i>…I’m okay with anything else happening.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Je suis le vôtre. J’étais toujours le vôtre, monsieur.”<br><u>I am yours. I have always been yours, sir.</u><br><br>“Oui. Tu es le mien.”<br><u>Yes, you are mine.</u></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>** ♥ BuddyRead with my lovely pal Sandyღ ♥ **</i>
</blockquote><br><br></span>

<div id="review_353822697" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/353822697" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/353822697?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cant-wait-cant-wait-cant-wait">cant-wait-cant-wait-cant-wait</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=net-galley-for-review">net-galley-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=bdsm-kink">bdsm-kink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=glbt">glbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer353822697" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4257086885609962578"><b>
  <blockquote>It is always by way of pain one arrives at pleasure. <br/>Marquis de Sade </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>This is another angsty walk on the wide side with our Original Sinners with three different story lines being told here – Wesley and Nora in Kentucky, Kingsley and Søren’s story in the past and also the present. It’s a painful story, in more ways than one – the physical pain that Søren needs to dish out and the emotional pain that all the characters have to endure to find some small semblance of pleasure and happiness.<br/><br/>This </span>
  <span id="freeText4257086885609962578" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>It is always by way of pain one arrives at pleasure. <br>Marquis de Sade </blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is another angsty walk on the wide side with our Original Sinners with three different story lines being told here – Wesley and Nora in Kentucky, Kingsley and Søren’s story in the past and also the present. It’s a painful story, in more ways than one – the physical pain that Søren needs to dish out and the emotional pain that all the characters have to endure to find some small semblance of pleasure and happiness.<br><br>This story is a tale of two Princes – Wes, Vanilla Prince of Kentucky, and Kingsley, much revered Prince of Darkness of the kinky underworld, with Søren and Nora taking their respective thrones as undisputed King and Queen but, for me, this book was all about Kinglsey Edge. Kingsley exudes charm, dominance and control and it’s so beautiful and such a pleasure to see the tortuous path that has brought him to the handsome, dandy dominant that he is today.<br><br>I felt his pain on so many levels, the losses and pain he has endured and continues to endure. His absolute devotion to Søren in their early days together was breathtaking as the brutal, primal, uncivilized savagery of the beginning of their relationship unfolds. It fills in a lot of details and answers a lot of questions left unanswered in The Angel.<br><br>I was quite shocked to find myself developing some sympathy for Søren, the only man in the Underworld to wear a collar but to belong to no one. To me, he’s always been this hardcore sadist who causes so much pain and resentment that I couldn’t understand the deep devotion that he engenders in those around him but, now, I think I do. It’s easy to imagine him as unfeeling and uncaring but nothing could be further from the truth but, outwardly, he is like winter – cold and distant.<br><br>Wes is his polar opposite – he is like summer and his touch burns Nora like the sun as they take their relationship further together. Nora thinks she is a better person when she is with Wes but I disagree. I prefer her when she is embracing her kink with the rest of the polyamorous sinners. I did enjoy their part of the novel but it took a lesser role for me, fading in comparison to the brilliance of Kingsley’s and Søren’s story.<br><br>So, I think fell even further in love with Kingsley reading this one although I hardly thought it was possible. <i>Kingsley – je t’aime et suis tienne et tu es mien.</i> The troubled Frenchman, girls, is mine!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380381645i/739008._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As always, it’s the richness of the writing that captivates me – Tiffany Reisz really has the most wonderful voice, ensnaring the reader right from the first few words and enforcing total immersion in her beautifully kinky world. I want to sink into it and never come up for air.<br><br>I have to say that this book ends on a <b>mother</b> of a cliffhanger and I sure hope that Tiff is writing fast as I now can’t stand to have to wait for The Mistress and I suspect that she may make us wait until 2013 for that one and everyone knows that the world is going to end on December 12th!<br><br>So, in the face of impending apocalypse, I have one final request. Please, please, please write a wicked scene for the unholy trinity of Nora, Kingsley and Søren. With details. Lots of details. Oh, and pictures. Too much? Ok, scratch the pictures if you must. Pretty please?? <a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381645ra/739009.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>4 angsty, tortured stars<br><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of Harlequin via NetGalley<br><br>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="4257086885609962578" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3316175952?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shile " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shile " href="/user/show/38826246-shile">Shile </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3316175952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13131156280639572603"><i>
  <b> The pianist was easily the most handsome young man Kingsley had ever seen in all his sixteen years. Vain as he was, Kingsley couldn’t deny he’d for once met his match there. But more than handsome, the pianist was also, in a way, as beautiful as the music he played.</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1588690651ra/29420118.gif' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is the best in this series and the hardest to rate. Left me speechless in the best possible way.<br/><br/>The story is told in two parts. <br/><br/>We have King and Soren's story, told in Past/ Present, this one gets infinity stars. What a bril</span>
  <span id="freeText13131156280639572603" style="display:none"><i>
  <b> The pianist was easily the most handsome young man Kingsley had ever seen in all his sixteen years. Vain as he was, Kingsley couldn’t deny he’d for once met his match there. But more than handsome, the pianist was also, in a way, as beautiful as the music he played.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1588690651ra/29420118.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is the best in this series and the hardest to rate. Left me speechless in the best possible way.<br><br>The story is told in two parts. <br><br>We have King and Soren's story, told in Past/ Present, this one gets infinity stars. What a brilliant emotional story. Is it requited or unrequited love? i am still trying to figure that out and still replaying the scenes between King and Soren over and over again. Their past is beautiful and painful. <br><br>Soren, OMG this guy, i love him, i really do but i want to shake him hard and i want to know his heart too. He made my heart ache and jump, my heart is still jumping.<br><br>King, my French man. Oh boy! My heart hurt for him. I love the young King, what a feisty little ladies man. Well until he met Soren. I wanted to hug him and tell him it will be okay, he will find another Soren, but that is a lie, there will never be another Soren. We are all in love with Soren. <br><br><i>
  <b>Søren looked away and took one step, but paused, turned around and shoved Kingsley hard into the wall of the chapel. This first kiss had been an apology of sorts from Søren, the second kiss an explanation. But this kiss, the third and final, it was an attack. Kingsley let Søren bite his lips, his tongue, dig his fingers into his throat.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588690651i/29420117.png" width="400" height="480" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gaaah! i am still hangover from the story of King and Soren. <br><br>The other part is Nora and Wes's story. Umm! This part i didn't care about at all. I don't know why Wes is even here. If he loves Nora like he says, He should accept Nora and all her kinky parts. Nora was still Nora and she made me laugh hard. I love this woman. I would give this part 2.5 stars. <br><br>Soren and King's story will stay with me forever. I hope to get answers to my many questions.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/698646765?book_show_action=true">Aug 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16165849-the-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer698646765" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1646866713108224238"><br/><b>
  <i>In all things involving Nora Sutherlin, proceed with caution</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>First off, let me say that this Series has intrigued me since I started it only last week. The first two books were outstanding. This one …..<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872669._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>The North, Past and Present – 5 stars<br/>The South – 4 stars<br/>The North, Past and Present – 6 stars<br/>The South – 3 stars<br/>The North, Past and Present – 7 stars<br/>The South …. Well, I would not give it 2 stars, it would be worth more than that I think.<br/><br/><br/>I seriously felt as if this book was written by 2 differe</span>
  <span id="freeText1646866713108224238" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>In all things involving Nora Sutherlin, proceed with caution</i>
</b><br><br><br>First off, let me say that this Series has intrigued me since I started it only last week. The first two books were outstanding. This one …..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872669._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The North, Past and Present – 5 stars<br>The South – 4 stars<br>The North, Past and Present – 6 stars<br>The South – 3 stars<br>The North, Past and Present – 7 stars<br>The South …. Well, I would not give it 2 stars, it would be worth more than that I think.<br><br><br>I seriously felt as if this book was written by 2 different authors. As soon as I hit The North, I was on a high. Down South, I just wanted to get in the Aston Martin and head up until I passed the Mason Dixie Line and made it back to the sanctuary of Maine and Connecticut…. And SØREN and KINGSLEY!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122045.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wes did absolutely nothing for me. Was not too pushed about him in the previous books but in this one I felt nothing for him – NADA, RIEN, INTET, NICHTS, NIETS, FAIC (I love that Irish word for “nothing” is "faic" – a word close to my heart)<br><br>Do ya get my drift?<br><br>The past and the relationship development between SØREN and KINGSLEY was amazing. I loved it. Loved reading about their first meeting, their interactions over the years. Kingsley, what a tortured soul. SØREN, I fell a little bit more in love with you, especially when Nora told us about you, during her stay in Kentucky – about 87% in – yeah, you guys know THAT scene. That was the only redeeming part of the South that I liked. I suppose she was trying to show the dichotomy of the different lifestyles, Wes and his picture perfect upbringing and Nora/SØREN/Kingsleys’ lives up North…<br><br><i>
  <b>Nora could do almost anything in her high heels…. He knew of one activity she couldn’t do in her high heels – run.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872670._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I am not going to say much more about the South, well one or two more things. <br><br><br>First of all, Wes is still a fucking Virgin, at aged 20. Was he seriously going to wait until it shriveled up and died! I mean, it was just by chance that Nora came back to him. OK, I was a Virgin when I was 20 but, girls, I lived in a village in the West of Ireland. I remember a girl a year older than me got “up the pole” as they would say in Ireland – yeah, awful, I know. The scandal! I remember my mother saying, I kid you not, “HOW COULD SHE DO THAT TO HER PARENTS?” Now, if that wouldn’t put the fear of God into you and make your Catholic guilt come to the fore, I don’t know what would. Plus there was not even a Pharmacy in our village. I remember the first time I went to buy condoms, myself and Himself went away for a weekend – of course did not tell my parents I was with him. I was friggin 21 at this stage. Went into a Pharmacy in a BIGGER town in the west of Ireland. The condoms were not even on display, like they are now, I had to ASK for them at the counter. I was mortified. The dirty look he gave me, I swear to God. Now, that I think of it, why was I the one going in to buy them and not Himself????<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122046.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>…. OK, the last bit of The South was good, the way it left all the possibilities open for THE MISTRESS. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122047.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, onwards and upwards to the NORTH … Loved every single, sadistic, sexy, sinful second of it. Truly wonderful writing. I could feel Kingsley’s anguish. I could feel his punishments. I wanted to take SØREN and hold him and tell him that nothing was his fault, he did not have to be like that, he had people who loved him….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122048.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122049.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>In concert, the piece began with the sound a whip crack… So beautiful … the music and the young man who played it. Kingsley listened to the piece, studied the pianist. He couldn’t decided which moved him more.</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872671._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Only one person had he ever loved more. But the one he loved more, he hated with equal passion. He wished that the mathematics of the world were like the mathematics of the heart – then his equal love and hate would mean he felt nothing instead of double.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872672.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>They comforted him, the stars did. The stars had been the only witness to that night. Did they remember it as well as he did?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872673.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>REVIENS. COME BACK</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872674.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428127ra/856385.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>GOD SAVED MY SOUL. YOU, HOWEVER, SAVED MY SANITY.</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872675.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>“I told you I’m French. Ever read the Marquis de Sade?”<br>He grinned from ear to ear and SØREN’s smile widened.<br>“Sometimes, I think I am him. I’ve read Machiavelli, too. <br><i>The Prince.</i> It is better to be feared than loved."<br>“And …” SØREN continued, “it’s safer to be feared than loved.”<br> <br><br><br><b>He’d died….. Died and been born again.<br>“My name is SØREN.”<br>“Je t’aime.”</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872676._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then we had, what I could only a clusterfuck moment at around 95%. Never anticipated that…. I swear I swore out loud in the office. My jaw dropped. It was fucking brilliant. Just confirmed that this author is way superior to a lot of writers out there.<br><br>“I said we were like Adam and Eve …. In hell.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122050.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I was going to drop a star because of the South but in the end I couldn’t. I was going to drop a star because there did not seem to be as many religious references that I absolutely loved in the first two books. But that was my preference in the first two books so it would not be fair to lower my rating because of that…<br><br>As with the other book, I could post more quotes I had highlighted, I could post more pictures that I think reflect the mood and subject matter of the book. <br><br>We had the PAST and the PRESENT…. Are we ready to find out what the FUTURE brings??<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380773326i/3122051.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>As a small child Wesley had heard the phrase "the wrath of God" in Church, and sat and wondered what had that meant, what that sounded like.<br>Now, he knew.</b><br><br>BRING ON ….<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380433600i/872677._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1646866713108224238" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/387361165?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>
