        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer387361165" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11490652361715112894"><br/>Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>5 Glowing, Shimmering Stars!! This book, this series, the writing, the story…all of it screams...UNIQUE…ORIGINAL</b>! It's found its way the top of my all-time favorites, as twisted and f*cked up as it is...I can't get enough!! <br/><br/>I’ve read a lot of great books this year and gotten hooked on some amazing series, but <b>nothing, nothing</b> comes close to the impact I’ve felt with <i>The Original Sinners</i> series, and book 3, <i>The Prince</i>, adds another layer of depth and complex</span>
  <span id="freeText11490652361715112894" style="display:none"><br>Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br><br><b>5 Glowing, Shimmering Stars!! This book, this series, the writing, the story…all of it screams...UNIQUE…ORIGINAL</b>! It's found its way the top of my all-time favorites, as twisted and f*cked up as it is...I can't get enough!! <br><br>I’ve read a lot of great books this year and gotten hooked on some amazing series, but <b>nothing, nothing</b> comes close to the impact I’ve felt with <i>The Original Sinners</i> series, and book 3, <i>The Prince</i>, adds another layer of depth and complexity to the characters and the plot! The title of this book alone holds more meaning than what I initially thought. <br><br>This one takes us back to when the original sinning begins, with alternating timelines and locations, and it transitions nicely from one scene to the next. We have Nora and Wesley in the present to, Soren, Nora and Kingsley in the past and present. <br><br>I thought I loved Soren and Kingsley, but after reading how they came to be, they’ve consumed me, and I <b>can’t get them out of my head!!!</b>. At times their story is harsh, hurtful, cruel and had me cringing, but the physical pain that’s inflicted is consensual, based on need and desire; Soren’s hunger to dish out pain and Kingsley craving to have it… and so it begins! What starts out as friendship, or rather what one can offer the other, becomes love and devotion. Soren and Kingsley’s story was my favorite part of the book! <br><br>Wesley and Nora explore their relationship, but I question whether it can ever be more than a passing curiosity for Nora. Wesley is such a sweet guy, I adore Nora, and I liked the time they spent together, but, but, but…you’ll have to decide for yourself...no more details from me!<br><br>There is an element of mystery and suspense in the plot, and will have you asking…could it be? Again the author surprises me, because each book lends itself to a different feel, they all connect, but read distinctive, not formulaic. She’s descriptive, without being boring; the dialogue is, witty, thoughtful and plentiful, Tiffany Riesz is an amazing, gifted author, and how fortunate we are to be able to explore the world and characters that she has created. <br><br>This books ends in a cliffhanger, and a final conversation, albeit a very short exchange of words, that speaks volumes…in my opinion it’s the writing on the wall about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[who Nora should be with, the one who she needs <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I can’t wait for the next book and just thinking about it makes my heart pound and gives me butterflies in my stomach. <br><br><b> Each of them rule their own domain, but who will reign supreme?? <br><br>Kingsley</b><br><a href="http://s1130.beta.photobucket.com/user/kparks823/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379778443i/379723.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Wesley</b><br> <a href="http://s1130.beta.photobucket.com/user/kparks823/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386950i/746646.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>“He didn’t even lay a hand on me. He didn’t have to. Broke me in half with words.” “He knows how to break you and yet leave you feeling more whole than you ever had before.”</i><br><br><b>or Soren</b><br><a href="http://s1130.beta.photobucket.com/user/kparks823/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386950i/746647.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><i>**ARC courtesy of Harlequin Mira via NetGalley!**</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer660321920" class="readable"
              >

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16165849-the-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443974257" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10441994420287439791"><br/><br/><b>FIVE+++++ "Can I have more Soren, please" STARS!<br/><br/><br/></b><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&current=more_zps08554b15.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/>This series is seriously epic! Love, love, love it. In fact, this is my favorite of the four books within TOS series. Third times a charm reading this one! <br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&current=tumblr_motm54nszT1s9uhkyo1_500_zps02dc95da.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395820ra/762501.gif' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>TOS just continues to get better with each installment. Spoiler alert <b>if you've not read the previous books in the series.....</b><br/><br/><b><br/>The Prince </b>is split back and forth between Soren and Kingsley's past and present and then also Nora and Wesley's present. Nora and Wesley are in Kentucky after So</span>
  <span id="freeText10441994420287439791" style="display:none"><br><br><b>FIVE+++++ "Can I have more Soren, please" STARS!<br><br><br></b><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=more_zps08554b15.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395820ra/762500.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This series is seriously epic! Love, love, love it. In fact, this is my favorite of the four books within TOS series. Third times a charm reading this one! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_motm54nszT1s9uhkyo1_500_zps02dc95da.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395820ra/762501.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>TOS just continues to get better with each installment. Spoiler alert <b>if you've not read the previous books in the series.....</b><br><br><b><br>The Prince </b>is split back and forth between Soren and Kingsley's past and present and then also Nora and Wesley's present. Nora and Wesley are in Kentucky after Soren asked Wes to care for her as there's a threat lurking in the shadows...a threat he fears will harm Nora. She's left her collar behind and is reuniting with the handsome 20-year old virgin she fell in love with but separated from a year or so ago. Wesley wants Nora to stay with him, The Prince of Kentucky but can Nora truly leave Soren behind? A life of no kink, no pain, for a life with no hiding, of luxury....of having a family....<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2014-12/7681BC64-B01C-4EC4-B6BC-954C51D7051E_zps34xchjzu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418947660i/12952967._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7681BC64-B01C-4EC4-B6BC-954C51D7051E_zps34xchjzu.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b><br>The Prince </b>gives us the much needed history of Kingsley and Soren. Having met as teenagers at Saint Ignatius Catholic boarding school, their story is torturous, violent yet full of unending loyalty and deep-seated love. Scenes with these two were gritty and intense. I found my heart racing, my teeth grinding. Both men coming from their fair share of pain, loss, or abuse coming together in the most unconventional yet functional way for them.....<br><br><br>I think the story,of Soren and Kingsley is seriously one of the more intense love stories I've read with two men. Their early days in the boarding school, where every student is frightened of the enigma that's "Stearns" yet Kingsley can't look away. Can't stop staring at this man...and Soren can't stand the staring!<br><br><br>Soren continues to be my swoon-worthy focus in this series (no judging!). His ability to be a committed spiritual man to his parish yet hides this all encompassing desire to inflict pain on the one (or two) he loves in order to GIVE love. How Ms Reisz can take such conflicting personal traits and make him swoon worthy is commendable.....and let me say, I SWOON for that sadistic yet angelic priest (talk about a conflict of terms). The character development of ALL these Original Sinners characters is stellar. The reader feels a part of their story, their lives, their struggles and pains. I think I could read this book a dozen times and still fall deeper in love with this book!<br><br>And that ending! The mother of all cliffies! Moving on to The Mistress!<br><br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><br><b>Some of my favorite quotes-<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=c5639cdd60b33fd48c796c1f5e4a708f_zpsf1c0640b.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395820i/762508._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=0f1ebbae2e26de37f75c54a85f1aff47_zpsf7129969.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395820i/762509._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=716442acc77ed947b719f46cbd938ede_zpsf29dd0b1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395820i/762510._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>And some Nora humor! Fan-girling!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=da654438cb67e2cd67bb15ed3dca4537_zpsb5ec8fcd.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395820i/762513._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=02bceadd25548205785012ac5a5eedde_zps41625dc8.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395820i/762514._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_402424034" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/402424034" />
    <a title="Sara " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5058304-sara"><img alt="Sara " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1439650883p2/5058304.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/402424034?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara " href="/user/show/5058304-sara">Sara </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=can-t-miss-book">can-t-miss-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=a-must-read">a-must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=stellar">stellar</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5058304-sara?shelf=arc-ng">arc-ng</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer402424034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3790513248404443155">I have said it before; The Siren sat me on my ass, The Angel kicked my ass and now The Prince? The Prince owns my ass. <br/><br/>I have been sucked in to the world of The Original Sinners for months; devouring everything that comes out getting to know them better. Just when I think I have a handle on who they are and what they may or may not do I am thrown to the ground gasping for air and reaching for the next story. <br/><br/>The Prince begins where we left off in The Angel. Nora has taken off her shoes and run s</span>
  <span id="freeText3790513248404443155" style="display:none">I have said it before; The Siren sat me on my ass, The Angel kicked my ass and now The Prince? The Prince owns my ass. <br /><br />I have been sucked in to the world of The Original Sinners for months; devouring everything that comes out getting to know them better. Just when I think I have a handle on who they are and what they may or may not do I am thrown to the ground gasping for air and reaching for the next story. <br /><br />The Prince begins where we left off in The Angel. Nora has taken off her shoes and run straight into the arms of Wesley. Søren is left alone with Kingsley who is more than ready to take advantage of the situation. While the Little One is away, our King wants to play.<br /><br />From the Prologue we get the voice of the thief who has stolen Nora’s file.The intrigue is deeply set and I will say after finishing the book; I went back and read it again. Trust me, do this. It will read completely different when you do. <br /><br />The alternating time lines and locations tell the story flawlessly. I knew with each heading where my mind and heart needed to be. From the North in The Past with Kingsley and Søren as teenagers meeting at Saint Ignatius; to the North in The Present thirty years later with them visiting ghosts of their pasts trying to unravel the mystery and the identity of the thief. Down to the South with Nora and Wesley living in a new world together trying to find their way and get what they need without being lost. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>NORTH <i>The Past:</i></u>
</b><br />The opportunity to be voyeur into the past of Søren and Kingsley as they meet was gorgeous. We know they had a relationship and they have a stronger bond even today that is beyond friendship. But seeing them, feeling through Kingsley the first time he saw Søren sitting at a piano playing Ravel, was magnificent. If you thought the first look at Søren in The Siren was majestic, this is ten times better. <br /><br />Through these chapters we see a different side of Søren; we see him yes as a young man but through Kingsley’s eyes he becomes much more of a ‘man’ than the enigma that we have seen him as. I learned so much about Søren that I have begun to understand him. Though we never get into his head, Kingsley let us see him thoroughly. I was fascinated by Søren in The Siren, I empathized with him in The Angel and now I have fallen hard for him. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"He smiled almost shyly and Kingsley understood it all – why Søren was so cold, so remote, why he could and did instill such fear in the hearts of everyone who came near him. He did it on purpose. He did it to keep them safe."</i>
</b><br /><br />Kingsley, oh the gorgeous Frenchman, I cannot think of him and not melt. The lengths that Søren and Kingsley go to for each other, to be with one another just about did my poor heart in. As secrets are revealed, stories are told and they are simply together my hand was permanently on my chest wanting more. <br /> <br /><b>
  <u>NORTH <i>The Present:</i></u>
</b><br />I love the way these chapters were set up. You see Kingsley and Søren in the past and then immediately you are in the present with them. You have the emotions and the history in your head. You are right there with them with every step, every conversation, every confession and every breathtaking moment between them that broke my heart and slowly stitched it back together again. Oh I loved these two in the past but bringing all of that forward immediately had me on my knees. <br />With Nora away with Wesley, Kingsley is not going to waste time now that he has Søren to himself. He is taking the opportunity to be with him while they investigate Nora’s stolen file. The trips back to the Saint Ignatius in the car…<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Lovely to know that I’m not the only one of us who engages in wishful thinking. Yes, she’ll come back to you…the day you come back to me."</i>
</b> <br /><br />There are so many moments in this I want to share. I have to say that there are four words, <b>FOUR WORDS</b> that made me drop the book with my hand to my heart and I had to remember to breathe. Four words that rocked my world and tore me apart while giving me so much hope and happiness it was overwhelming. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>SOUTH:</u>
</b><br />Oh my poor romantic heart! I am forever on Team Wesley and seeing him this way was beyond my wildest dreams and fantasies. Wesley bringing Nora home, standing up for her, showing her his world and wanting to share it with her had me sighing at least a dozen times in each chapter. <br /><br />Nora was grounded here; there is something about Wesley that changes her and being in his world is definitely altering yet she is still the witty Nora we have come to love. The pure need and love between these two was what I have been waiting, hoping and wishing for. Neither of them holds anything back…<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Wesley’s absence from her life has been a void no amount of sex or money or kink or fame had been able to fill."</i>
</b> <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"It’s sad when a Thoroughbred gets hurts in a race. But when Søren hurts you, I die inside."</i>
</b> <br /><br />Nora and Wesley together; that is it, it has to be enough just to say that. One whole book of them being apart was torture. I am taking them anyway I can and holy hell is it something to see.<br /> <br />There is so much I want to say about this but I just can’t. I can’t go on without spoiling it and I don’t do spoilers. I feel that writing this has spoiled it enough, even for me and I have read it twice and a couple handfuls of scenes at least a dozen times. <br /><br />I was absolutely blown away by The Prince. I finished it two weeks ago and I cannot let it go. I hear songs, see pictures and am immediately drawn back into the story. The mystery of who stole Nora’s file is there throughout each page and I was stunned when I realized who it was. Jaw on the floor stunned and then the massive cliff hanger ending? A whole party of questions started dancing around my head and they will never hear the last call alert. <br /><br />There was so much emotion in this book that I dare you, I double dog dare you not to feel when you read it. It’s impossible; unless you are dead inside, lack a heart, an open mind and the imagination to go where you must. <br /><br /><i>*ARC provided by Harlequin MIRA via NetGalley.</i><br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3790513248404443155" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_366488551" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/366488551?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=arc-netgalley">arc-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=explicit">explicit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=november-2012">november-2012</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer366488551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3453856193485205014"><i>Fuck it.</i> No amount of stars can truly describe how brilliant this story is. <br/><br/><b>…I firmly resolve, with the help of Your Grace, to sin no more and to avoid the near occasion of sin ~ Act of Contrition</b><br/><br/>Holy shit. Holy shit, HOLY FUCKING SHIT! This was brilliant. I’m in utter awe. No amount of words and no amount of stars can describe how much I love this book/series. With each book, Mistress Tiffany keeps getting better and better. I really don’t know how she does it. To me, nothing in the story was p</span>
  <span id="freeText3453856193485205014" style="display:none"><i>Fuck it.</i> No amount of stars can truly describe how brilliant this story is. <br><br><b>…I firmly resolve, with the help of Your Grace, to sin no more and to avoid the near occasion of sin ~ Act of Contrition</b><br><br>Holy shit. Holy shit, HOLY FUCKING SHIT! This was brilliant. I’m in utter awe. No amount of words and no amount of stars can describe how much I love this book/series. With each book, Mistress Tiffany keeps getting better and better. I really don’t know how she does it. To me, nothing in the story was pretty or simple, but she manages to completely ensnare me with her words. With her words, the characters she created become real and raw. You start to connect with them. You feel their pain, both physical and emotional. You feel their longing and yearning. She just knows how to paint a beautifully raw story and you can’t help but be immersed in this world. I didn’t ever want this to end. <br><br><b>
  <i>“When Jesus tells us to love God with our heart, soul and mind, He is telling us that they are three and one, just as the Godhead.” ~ Stearns</i>
</b><br><br>The Prince is intense, no doubt. The characters I thought I knew, I didn’t know at all. This book told the three different stories: Søren/Kingsley (Past &amp; Present) and Wesley/Nora (Present). Each story has their own feeling and vibe; their own story to tell. However, the deeper you get into the book as a whole, you start to see patterns emerge and each story starts to collide into each other to create this masterpiece. <br><br><b>NORTH</b><br><br><b>
  <i>The crown his parents had placed on his head, even naming him Kingsley, although a less French name had never existed…he’d take off that crown and lay it at Søren‘s feet. And the prince would become a servant and the king a commoner all night long. </i>
</b><br><br><i>Mercy. Merci.</i> Where do I begin to express my feelings towards Søren and Kingsley? I’ve always been hesitant in giving my heart to Søren, but after getting to know him more through the eyes of Kingsley, I can honestly say that I love him. Søren and Kingsley’s relationship, especially as teenagers, shattered me. Their relationship was intense. It was raw, painful, but full of love; it was utterly beautiful to behold. Fuck. My love for Søren and Kingsley cannot be described. They exposed so many things and reading about their struggles and their coming together was so intense. I had to occasionally put the book down because it was overwhelming and I felt it all over my body. My heart was exposed and both men marched right in. Søren and Kingsley…<i>fuck</i>. I love them.<br><br><b>SOUTH</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s always a good day when the Prince of Kentucky and the Queen of the Underground come calling.”</i>
</b><br><br>**SIGH** My Wesley ♥♥♥♥. <b>
  <u>I love him.</u>
</b> Can you tell? After the ending of The Angel, I couldn’t wait to dive into this. I was on pins and needles reading their story. They have been apart for fifteen long months. How will their relationship change? Will it flourish or is my Wesley headed for another heartbreak?<br><br>Wow. What I wouldn’t give to have been Nora in this story. To have Wesley in my arms, worshiping me…**sigh**…Oh Wesley, you certainly have haunted my dreams. Oh. My. God. The intimate scenes he shared with Nora just popped in my head. Fuck me. He has certainly grown into quite a man. **SIGH** I just fucking love him to pieces. When he hurts, I hurt. There were times where I couldn’t understand Nora and just wanted to flog her. Not that she didn’t outright adore him, but I know how he feels about her and I just wanted…I don’t know, a little more. Then again, I’m highly emotional when it comes to my Wesley. It’s my problem, I know. He has the power to make or break me. I beg you, please take care of him in the next book. He deserves to be happy. <br><br><b>To Mistress Tiffany:</b> Thank you so much for writing and creating this brilliant series. This series has become one of my all-time favorites. God has blessed you with such talent and I’m so thankful you use it to create this world. This world you masterfully created is so beautiful and so sensual. I love it. Nothing has compared to it. All these characters are embedded in my heart and soul. I will be anxiously waiting for the release of The Mistress &amp; The Priest. <br><br>Many thanks to Harlequin and NetGalley for providing this ARC. <br><br>-----<br><b>

    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/449242869?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16165849-the-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=unforgettables">unforgettables</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=books-with-an-edge">books-with-an-edge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=continuing-plot">continuing-plot</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449242869" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10134957698346841444"><b>
  <i>For over ten years after he and Søren had parted company, Kingsley had lived the most dangerous life he could. He ran from death the way he’d run that night from Søren— in the hopes he’d get caught and taken. Not until they reunited had Kingsley found a purpose in his life again, a reason to live.</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627231._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>Underneath Søren, Kingsley came more alive than he ever felt on top of any girl. He loved his girls, had loved them all. But this was more than love. He couldn’t think of the word for it— not l’a</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10134957698346841444" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>For over ten years after he and Søren had parted company, Kingsley had lived the most dangerous life he could. He ran from death the way he’d run that night from Søren— in the hopes he’d get caught and taken. Not until they reunited had Kingsley found a purpose in his life again, a reason to live.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627231._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>Underneath Søren, Kingsley came more alive than he ever felt on top of any girl. He loved his girls, had loved them all. But this was more than love. He couldn’t think of the word for it— not l’amour, not la passion.... la vie. It was the closest word to what he felt that he could find. <br>La vie. <br>Life.<i></i></i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627233._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>Nora was lawless, unmanageable, uncontrollable. You told her one thing, she did everything but that. She laughed when others cried. Danced when others sat. She clawed her way to the top and didn’t even chip a nail on the way up. No one could break her. No one could handle her. No one could shut her up.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764764._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"You are blessed indeed to have such a great woman in your life. We are mere princes, you and I. But she is a queen."<br></i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379797101i/627234._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Prince starts off where The Angel left off. Nora has gone to Kentucky to be with Wesley, and Soren and Kingsley are attempting to figure out who had stolen the file from Kingsley's estate and is a potential threat.<br><br>Told in three parts, we get a deeper and darker look into the past and present relationship between Soren and Kingsley, as well as the one between Nora and Wes.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764767.jpg" width="80" height="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>The Past</b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764767.jpg" width="80" height="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The past takes us back to 30 years ago when Soren and Kinglsey just met. I can't say that learning more about Kingsley endeared him to me any more. Half the time he came off as a surly and spoiled boy, the other half as obsessively in love with Soren. <br><br>Soren is still just as terrifying as a boy, as he is in present time. He terrifyes everyone from the students to the staff. Only Kingsley sees something beyond the cold exterior.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“You aren’t afraid of me right now.” A statement, not a question, and yet Kingsley heard the question underneath the words. Why? <br>“There’s nothing you could do to me now that I wouldn’t want.” <br>Stearns looked Kingsley up and down, as if he realized an alien lay beneath him instead of a person. <br>“What are you?” Stearns asked him the same question Kingsley had asked him, but Kingsley had a much simpler answer. <br>“I’m French.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>The relationship between them is dark, and twisted, and at times reading it almost made me cringe. Though I have to admit, I couldn't picture it any other way.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764768._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764767.jpg" width="80" height="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>The Present</b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764767.jpg" width="80" height="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Taking place in present time, takes Soren and Kingsley to investigate the person that is threatening them. After receiving a picture of the two of them as boys in school, they realize that the threat is much closer to them than either of them thought. They travel back to the school where everything first started. Kingsley is still trying to get over his unrequitted love for Soren, and jealous resentment of Nora.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Søren told her everything and gave her everything. And then she’d had the audacity to walk away from it all. Søren laid out feasts for her that she merely picked at, while Kingsley lapped up the crumbs that fell to the floor.</b>
</blockquote><br>Soren is still the stuff of sadistic legends in the underground.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764769._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>After finishing this book, I can say I am completely and 100% team Soren. I cannot picture Nora with anyone else. Though he still terrifies the living crap out of me, I have to say that getting a deeper look inside the man that he is helped me understand him a lot more.<br><br>There is also the mystery of the threat that has come up with the theft of Nora's file. More and more threats keep popping up, that reveal that whoever this threat is knows a lot about everything that has to do with Soren. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764767.jpg" width="80" height="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>The South</b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396624i/764767.jpg" width="80" height="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The South brings us the relationship of Nora and Wesley. This was my favorite part of the book. Nora was still same old Nora, but Wesley does seem to bring around a different side to her.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"I know how to tie knots that sailors who’ve spent half their lives at sea have never even heard of. I can pick locks that would stump half the cat burglars in New York. I can slice a Post-It note in half with the tip of a bullwhip. I can get any kinky man in the world to drop to his knees, kiss my feet and confess his darkest sins to me just for the pleasure of having me punish him for them. But, Wesley… I do not know who to be with somebody like you. A sweet, kind, vanilla virgin has me stumped. It’s been fifteen months since the last time we tried, and I still haven’t figured it out."</b>
</blockquote><br>The relationship between them was incredibly sweet, and was the perfect light from the darkness that was Soren and Kingsley. The love scenes between them were equal parts sweet<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764770.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and it seems like young Wesley finally did allow his sexy side to come a little too<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the way he rubbed off on Nora without really changing who she is.<br><blockquote>"Nora, have you never cuddled before?" <br>"Not like this. Here. You lay on your back. I’ll lay on you."<br>"Fine. Fine…" Wesley rolled onto his back and Nora collapsed onto his chest. He let out a puff of air as she scrambled into position. <br>"Are you made of lead?" <br>"I’m solid muscle and evil. Stop bitching and cuddle me."</blockquote><br><br>Now as for the ending....AHHHHHHH!!!!! That fucking cliffhanger! Holy.Effin.SHIT! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396624ra/764772.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10134957698346841444" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1737439198" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1737439198" />
    <a title="Saint Monique" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40572117-saint-monique"><img alt="Saint Monique" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559130947p2/40572117.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1737439198?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saint Monique" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saint Monique" href="/user/show/40572117-saint-monique">Saint Monique</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780263905823" href="/book/show/16141094-the-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=punish-me-with-pleasure">punish-me-with-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=omg-i-am-in-love-with-this-book">omg-i-am-in-love-with-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40572117-saint-monique?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1737439198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5307590903360370147"><b>ALL THE <i>'BEAUTIFULLY HEARTBREAKING, STUNNINGLY GORGEOUS AND WONDERFULLY AMAZING'</i> STARS</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Always…” Søren glanced away again, glanced upward, and sighed. “I’ve always wanted to believe God made me this way for a reason.”<br/>“Je suis la raison.”<br/>Søren exhaled slowly. He ran a hand up Kingsley’s arm to his shoulder. Cupping the side of his neck, he brought his mouth down to Kingsley’s. Such a gentle kiss, so intimate yet careful.<br/>“Ma raison d’être,” Søren whispered, and Kingsley shivered with need.</blockquote>
</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText5307590903360370147" style="display:none"><b>ALL THE <i>'BEAUTIFULLY HEARTBREAKING, STUNNINGLY GORGEOUS AND WONDERFULLY AMAZING'</i> STARS</b><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Always…” Søren glanced away again, glanced upward, and sighed. “I’ve always wanted to believe God made me this way for a reason.”<br>“Je suis la raison.”<br>Søren exhaled slowly. He ran a hand up Kingsley’s arm to his shoulder. Cupping the side of his neck, he brought his mouth down to Kingsley’s. Such a gentle kiss, so intimate yet careful.<br>“Ma raison d’être,” Søren whispered, and Kingsley shivered with need.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>First read: 25 Mar 2017 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br>Re-read: 7 Jan 2020 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟 <br><br>I don’t even know where to start or how to express my feelings. Maybe it's a cliché to say that this book made me speechless but it's an honest truth. I have no other words but some nonsensical babbling about how this story is so beautiful it hurts. (Yes, pun definitely intended.)<br><br><i>Warning: the usual stuff. Possible spoilers because I get carried away when Sinners are concerned, a lot of mushy moments, too many quotes and me raving about how much I adore Kingsley.</i><br><br>If you are familiar with my obsession with Original Sinners then you must also know that my heart and soul belong to the one and only Kingsley Edge.<br><br>Now imagine the joy I felt when I was reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704485.The_Prince__The_Original_Sinners___3_" title="The Prince (The Original Sinners, #3) by Tiffany Reisz" rel="nofollow noopener">The Prince</a> for the first time and discovered that 2/3 of the book is in King's POV. Paradise, I tell you. However, since back then I only started to warm up to Søren, I wasn’t wholly convinced by their love story. Sure I loved to read about them but I didn't really care much about them being together or not.<br><br>And now re-reading the series with the knowledge of the whole story (with all the possible novellas included) I'm finally experiencing the beauty of Søren and Kingsley's love.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I loved you because of the Ravel. Had you played any other piece I would have thought you merely handsome and fascinating.”<br>Søren gazed up at the sky. “Then I’m glad I played it.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>It's interesting how I see everything with different eyes now. Where I saw cruelty before, I see tenderness, where I thought was only indifference, I know it's actually love. Such a brilliant narrative, revealing their secrets and emotions layer by layer.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You stared at me constantly, followed me everywhere I went. You watched me sleep, Kingsley.”<br>“How did you know that?” Kingsley shivered as Søren’s laugh rippled through the woods.<br>“I watched you watch me.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>***********************************<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I hated how you stared at me.” Søren raised his hand and laid it on Kingsley’s shoulder. He moved his hand up Kingsley’s neck and pressed his thumb into the hollow of his throat.<br>“And why is that?”<br>“Because,” Søren said, bending his regal head the four inches that separated them, “it made it impossible for me to stare back.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Like every love story in Sinners, this one is unconventional as well. If you pair up hardcore sadist with hardcore masochist you can expect a whole lot of pain. And I mean, really brutal kind. I have to admit I actually winced one or two times at my first reading and all I wanted to do was put Kingsley somewhere safe and maybe read him a bedtime story and sing him a lullaby. But now I perfectly understand he was having the time of his life.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Pain with every touch. Pain with every kiss. Pain with every beat of his heart. Kingsley loved this pain.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>As I already mentioned, it took me some time to sort my mind about Søren. But knowing his side of the story I finally got to realize that the more he's cold on the outside, the more he's melting on the inside. And now imagine how wonderful reading experience was seeing him with his ice-cold walls around him and knowing that in truth, on the inside his love is burning hot.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I thought you were the most beautiful creature on God’s earth,” Kingsley confessed. “I would have been an atheist but for you proving to me that both heaven and hell were real, even if they existed only when I was with you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Was that enough of me gushing about Kingsley and Søren? No? All right, one more quote.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>The kiss had seemed less personal than the touch. He’d kissed his mother, his sister, his father, his friends. All the French kissed all the time. A kiss was nothing. But to touch fingertips to another’s lips…so erotic, so possessive, so intimate.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Before I completely forget. There was also some part of the book about Nora and Wesley. But I'm sure you all liked better to listen about Søren and King, right? Honestly, the two of them had my entire attention and devotion in this book.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Je suis le vôtre. J’étais toujours le vôtre, monsieur.”<br>“Oui. Tu es le mien.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><i>B(R)R with my Sinner Ladies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/52957386-melanie-a" rel="nofollow noopener">Melanie</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58429822-ursy" rel="nofollow noopener">Ursy</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14379473-leila" rel="nofollow noopener">Leila</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66575688-whitney" rel="nofollow noopener">Whitney</a>.</i><br><br>***********************************<br><b>Reading Original Sinners. Do not disturb!<br>If you need me, I'm in a Rolls-Royce with my Kingsley.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1576502181i/28620935._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1576502181i/28620936._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5307590903360370147" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3161266645" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3161266645" />
    <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers"><img alt="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581473939p2/74622641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3161266645?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers" href="/user/show/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers">Starr (AKA Bam Bam) Rivers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36172355-the-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=erotic-bdsm">erotic-bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=contem-new-adult-romance">contem-new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74622641-starr-aka-bam-bam-rivers?shelf=dom-sub">dom-sub</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3161266645" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14144327593513277877">So, this one is 3.5 stars, and the stars are all for Kingsley and Soren, 1.5 off bc of Nora, see notes below.<br/><br/>Here's what I know for sure:<br/>* King truly loves Soren. As a soul-mate in a way. He loves Nora more like a pet. King is very clear who he wants most in life, tho he's fond of various people, including Juliette. <br/><br/>I am uncertain about pretty much everything else.<br/><br/>Does Soren TRULY love Nora? I feel like after this book it has a tone of "fatherly" love. He "cherishes" her, but does he obsessively</span>
  <span id="freeText14144327593513277877" style="display:none">So, this one is 3.5 stars, and the stars are all for Kingsley and Soren, 1.5 off bc of Nora, see notes below.<br /><br />Here's what I know for sure:<br />* King truly loves Soren. As a soul-mate in a way. He loves Nora more like a pet. King is very clear who he wants most in life, tho he's fond of various people, including Juliette. <br /><br />I am uncertain about pretty much everything else.<br /><br />Does Soren TRULY love Nora? I feel like after this book it has a tone of "fatherly" love. He "cherishes" her, but does he obsessively love her? Is she truly his equal or is he really just his property that he covets? I do think he's very loyal to people, both to King back when they were boys, to his sister who raped him when he was 11, and to Nora, because he hasn't been with anyone sexually since he met her. (And from 18 to 34). That's pretty devoted. And we know from book 2 that Soren CAN be tempted. Probably not to that point, but he can be tempted.<br /><br />BUT. He can't resist King. He tries and tries and perhaps the guilt of King's sister destroyed what they had together, but in the end he still can't resist King. <br /><br />This makes me think Soren and King are meant to be soul-mates and Nora got in between them (and so did the sister). <br /><br />Which makes me dislike Nora even more and - yeah Nora, go off with Wesley (but really, that will never work, not unless Wes suddenly became the king of kink. And in that case, I doubt Nora will love him any more.) <br /><br />Nora's love for Wes is the most inauthentic I feel like. Most forced. Conversely, Wes' love of Nora is just as forced to me. He's a virgin with a puppy love first crush. She's a kinky switch who loves the novelty. She will get tired of him and his world and he will become resentful of her strange ways. It's never going to work.<br /><br />BUT I really hope she doesn't go back to Soren! I want Soren and King to get together so bad! Get together FOREVER! They don't need a thing to play with and share between them. Or if they do, it can be some other woman they don't "love" - not Nora. <br /><br />Anyway, read the reviews of book 4, it seems focused on Nora. Since I literally skimmed those parts in this book (and they still irritated me), I will skip book 4. Wonder when I can finally get my King and Soren ending...<br /><br />And if there's no such a thing, then I guess I'm done with this series.<br /><br />Annnnnnnddddd, not planning to read the 4th book bc of all the spoilers I read. Nothing to bring me to King and Soren HEA. So. Can't fork over another $6.99+tax<br /><br />Kinda disappointing if I think about it</span>
  <a data-text-id="14144327593513277877" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17704565967632532788"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Je suis la raison.”<br/>I am the reason.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>Totally unexpected turn of events and one hell of Cliffhanger made this yet another mindblowing, unconventional love story delivered by Tiffany Reisz. <br/><br/>I wont go into the details of this story or the characters since it’s already been established that the author can never go wrong on both the aspects but let me just say one name which holds highest respect in my heart and soul, for being epitome of submission and that’s The King of the Underground- </span>
  <span id="freeText17704565967632532788" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Je suis la raison.”<br>I am the reason.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>Totally unexpected turn of events and one hell of Cliffhanger made this yet another mindblowing, unconventional love story delivered by Tiffany Reisz. <br><br>I wont go into the details of this story or the characters since it’s already been established that the author can never go wrong on both the aspects but let me just say one name which holds highest respect in my heart and soul, for being epitome of submission and that’s The King of the Underground- <b>Kingsley edge.</b><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I have nothing in me that you cannot break. <br>I would let you destroy me, and then <br>I would resurrect myself from my own ashes <br>for the honor of being destroyed by you again.”</b>
    <i></i>
  </i>
</blockquote>Getting to know King was ecstasy in itself. There are so many amazing characters in this series but King stands out from the rest because the way he <s>loves</s> worships, his need to submit, his burning desire, the passion to please and underlying dedication towards his master was breathtaking. I personally feel honored to have witnessed this beautiful young man fighting his battle of rage/lust in his new found love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419687864i/13113016._SX540_.jpg" width="410" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> Buddy read with lovely Eda♥</i><br></span>

<div id="review_663781518" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/663781518" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/663781518?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=my-top-reads">my-top-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer663781518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2093118272367494936"><i>
  <b>"I watched you watch me."</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857920.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>We have the North.... past and present with Kinglsey, Soren & Nora<br/> <br/>We have the South..... the present with Wes and Nora.</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>What will we have in future....??????</b>
</i><br/><br/>The Prince turns things upside down for me......<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857921._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Not only is this a highly erotic book with all kinds of kinkiness but its a wonderful passionate love story and a spectacular<i> 'who done it???'</i> <br/><br/><blockquote> <i><b>It has everything......</b></i>
</blockquote><br/>All the painful delicate issues you could imagine; difficult topics and themes are layered int</span>
  <span id="freeText2093118272367494936" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"I watched you watch me."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857920.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>We have the North.... past and present with Kinglsey, Soren &amp; Nora<br> <br>We have the South..... the present with Wes and Nora.</b><br><br><i>
  <b>What will we have in future....??????</b>
</i><br><br>The Prince turns things upside down for me......<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857921._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Not only is this a highly erotic book with all kinds of kinkiness but its a wonderful passionate love story and a spectacular<i> 'who done it???'</i> <br><br><blockquote> <i><b>It has everything......</b></i>
</blockquote><br>All the painful delicate issues you could imagine; difficult topics and themes are layered into this series. They're revealed through a fabulous story that's utterly compelling.... <br><br><i>
  <b>There's a thief......who is it??? </b>
</i>I had many suspects..... I'm not going to list them....my gut instinct was right and I don't want to give you any clues.... just go with the flow.... there's one major clue ...... it's so exciting.... I love it!!!!!!<br><br>******<br><br><br>♥<i>Who experiences the greatest love of all....???</i><br>♥Who does your heart belong to...??? <br>♥Who do you want to see have their desires and dreams completely fulfilled?? <br><br><i>
  <b>Just some of the thoughts going round in my head...</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380298614i/685986._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>There are parts to this story that are quite brutal, hard to understand and rationalize, but there are also extremely tender moments; a touch, a look or a thought from a character brings you back from being uncomfortable to melting at two peoples affection and adoration for each other.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857922.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>In places The Prince is truly beautiful.... the emotions it evokes from the characters are so very powerful it translates with equal force to the reader..... that's how it felt to me anyway.<br><br><br><i>Nora is still on her man journey and taking me with her all the way....</i><br><br><i>
  <b>"... I missed who I was with you..."</b>
</i><br><br>Nora likes who she is with Wes, her summer, <i>
  <b> "...you make me a different person, a better person..." </b>
</i> This is the most articulate book I have ever read in describing how people can love more than one person, and in different ways.<br><br>Wes and Nora made me feel tingly <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ when they finally made the move.....when Wes said....<i><b>"Let's go to bed." </b></i>I swooned...  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>♥<i>Who is the real Nora....???<br>♥Are we products of our experiences???<br>♥Can you be anyone you choose to be....??? <br>♥Has destiny and fate already laid a path for you......??? <br>♥Do you have to choose...??? </i><br><br>♥<i>
  <b>Can you have everything????</b>
</i><br><br><br>In the South I saw a taste of what I wanted for Nora's character, what I thought would be the ideal..... I loved it, it made me warm inside, but at the same time, I'm not sure that's really what I want for her anymore.... or that it's the best for her.... confused..??? I certainly am......<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857923._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He is in fact the best man on earth,<br> not that anyone ever believes me<br> when I tell them that." </i>
  </b>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>"Anyone who knows him<br> at all loves him. And if they<br> don't love him, then they do <br>not know him."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857925._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>We learn a lot more about Soren and Kinglsley's time at Saint Ignatius. Their friendship, their connection... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ their love, their kinks  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It was all to last a lifetime, the friends were to be forever entwined.<br><br>We gain further understanding of all the 'loves'..... There are reasons for everything and Tiffany Reisz has so masterfully weaved them into this series.... <i>
  <b>weaved them and blown our minds.</b>
</i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>
    <i>"They had dreamed of such a girl as this...... He had found her and he would share her." ~ Kingsley</i>
  </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428632i/857926._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>♥<i> "When you love somebody, they own you whether you're kinky or not." </i> <b>
  <i>.......True ♥ </i>

  <i>P.S. I adore Kingsley ♥ </i>
</b> <br><br><br>BR with my lovely Deanna, Stella and Sarah..... xxxxx<br>And lots of support from Mo &amp; Irene.... <span id="freeTextContainer13283423610730843181"><b>5 I Want Nora's Men Stars!! </b><br/><p> Ms Reisz has done it again!! This series is just blowing my mind and I'm ashamed that it took me sooooooo long to pick this series up to read!!</p><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404772612ra/10280586.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><p>This story is told uniquely, in that Ms. Reisz takes us on a journey to the North with Soren and Kinsley. We also travel to the South with Nora and Wesley. Where some may have loved one area more than the other, this whore loved being in both destinations.</p><br/><p><b>NORTH</b><br/> So let's travel to the North first, shall we, where Ms. Reisz take</p></span>
  <span id="freeText13283423610730843181" style="display:none"><b>5 I Want Nora's Men Stars!! </b><br><p> Ms Reisz has done it again!! This series is just blowing my mind and I'm ashamed that it took me sooooooo long to pick this series up to read!!</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404772612ra/10280586.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>This story is told uniquely, in that Ms. Reisz takes us on a journey to the North with Soren and Kinsley. We also travel to the South with Nora and Wesley. Where some may have loved one area more than the other, this whore loved being in both destinations.</p><br><p><b>NORTH</b><br> So let's travel to the North first, shall we, where Ms. Reisz takes us back in time to where it all began with Soren and Kingsley.</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404772612ra/10280587.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>I can not even begin to tell you how awesome it was to see a young Soren and Kingsley. Ms. Reisz lets us peek at these young men before Soren became a priest. Of course they both already have been damaged by tragedies in their lives but it was those incidents that helped build them into the men we know in the present. Trust me when I say, young Soren and Kingsley were fucking hot together!!</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394554ra/759637.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404773806ra/10280814.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404758267i/10278918._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404773806i/10280815._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>Back in the present, here up North, things are getting a tad creepy as a mysterious picture shows up from Soren's and Kingsley's past, along with the missing file of one, Mistress Nora Sutherlin. Someone, a ghost from their past, is out to hurt them. Soren and Kingsley go on an investigative adventure to find the mystery person wanting to cause them problems. Who will piece it all together and will they find this ghost before anyone gets hurt?</p><br><p><b>SOUTH</b><br>Down South, we follow Prince of Kentuckey, Wesley Railey, and Nora Sutherlin as they travel to his kingdom, where they'll <i>meet the parents</i>.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400033444ra/9625660.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></p><p>As one might imagine, meeting Mr &amp; Mrs Railey was quite comical, thanks to Nora's smart mouth. Mr. Railey does know all about Mistress Nora's profession as a Dominatrix and let's just say he wasn't too happy about it. I gotta say, though, that Prince Wesley really took a stance and did not let Daddy intimidate him. Wesley and Nora have a few adventures of their own while on the Railey estate. I enjoyed seeing a glimpse of what Nora's life would be like if she doesn't go back to <b>Him</b>.....he who should not be named!!</p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404778489i/10281179.jpg" width="350" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404758267i/10278919._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>Nora and her Wesley....<b>FINALLY</b> make love because let's face it, that's what it is. It was beautifully vanilla and so worth the wait. Let me tell you, these two definitely make up for lost time......it was so damn sizzling that I saw smoke coming out of my Kindle.....true story!!</p><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402673851ra/9970275.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404779534ra/10281808.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><p>The Prince flipped back and forth between North and South until finally the two merged, leaving one hell of a cliffhanger!!! I did guess who "the ghost" was but this entire book is just pure brilliance!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400105185ra/9635657.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b>So glad I had the AWESOME WHORES in the BR group to hold my hand during this one!!</b><br><br></p></span>
